# Automatic Tax Category IDs and Names

Modified on: Wed, 10 Sep, 2025 at 12:42 AM

This document provides an overview of the tax categories available in GoHighLevel (GHL). These categories help ensure accurate tax calculations across products, services, and subscriptions.

### **Overview**

In GHL, taxes can be applied to transactions, subscriptions, and products using **Tax Category IDs** and **Tax Category Names**. On the UI, businesses can select the Tax Category Name, which corresponds to a unique Tax Category ID on the backend used for calculations and reporting. Proper assignment ensures accurate tax handling and compliance with local and international tax regulations.

### **How to Use Tax Categories**

1. Assigning Categories: When creating or editing a product or default for a sub-account, select the appropriate Tax Category Name from the available options on the UI.

2. Calculating Taxes: GHL uses the associated Tax Category Name to apply the correct tax rate based on the customerâ€™s location and your configured nexus addresses.

3. For APIs, use the Category IDs and Category Names local to GoHighlevel.


### **Notes**

- Regularly review your tax categories to stay compliant with updates to local tax laws.

- If a tax category does not apply to a transaction, select "Non-Taxable" or the relevant **Tax Category Name** to ensure no tax is applied.
